 				$(document).ready(function(){
 					var $cookieConsentPopupScript = $("#cookie-consent-script-popup");

   <script>
    function getCookie(cname) {
             var name = cname + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                 if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
             }
             return "";
         }
         function redirect(redirectToURL) {
             var redirect = 'null';
             if (redirectToURL != null && redirectToURL.trim().length > 0) {
                 redirect = redirectToURL;
             }
             if (window.location.hash) {
                 redirect += window.location.hash;
             }
             if (redirect != 'null') {
                 window.location.replace(redirect);
             }
         }

      <script>
       var socialShareData;
     
 	if (showLanguageSelector) {
 		prepareLanguageSelector(navigationData.languageSelectorData);
 	}    
 	prepareTerritorySelector(navigationData.territorySelectorData);
     prepareHamburger(navigationData.hamburgerData);
     prepareBreadcrumb(navigationData.breadcrumbData);
     socialShareData = navigationData.socialShareData;
     function createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             var languageListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#language-selector-template").html());
             $("#menuAdditional .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             languageSelectorData.isMobile=true;
             $("#menuAdditionalMobile .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
         }
     }
 
     function  prepareLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             //render alternate language div on page only if alternate language present on page/slim-header.
             createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData);
         }
     }
 
     function prepareTerritorySelector(territories){
         if (territories && territories.length > 0) {
             var territoryListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#territory-selector-template").html());
             $(".territory-dropdown").append(territoryListTemplate(territories));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareHamburger(hamburgerData){
         if ((hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks && (hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0
                 || hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0)) || (hamburgerData.levelOneLinks && hamburgerData.levelOneLinks.length > 0)) {
 
            
             if(hamburgerData.sectionTitle){
                 hamburgerData.hasSectionTitle=true;
             }
            // modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary);
             //modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.secondary);
             var hamburgerTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-template").html());
             //$("div.breadcrumb-main").append(hamburgerTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             $(".hamburger-menu .col-sm-8").append(hamburgerTemplate(hamburgerData));
             //populate levelOne links of hamburger
             var hamburgerLevelOneTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-levelOne-template").html());
             $("#LevelOneLinks").prepend(hamburgerLevelOneTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
             //populate hamburger for mobile
             var hamburgerMobileTemplate= Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-mobile-template").html());
             $(".hamburger-submenu--mobile .panel-group").append(hamburgerMobileTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
         }else {
             //if levelOne or LevelTwo or LevelThree Links are not present, hamburger button should not be shown.
             $("#dropdownTrigger_lg").remove();
             $("#navBar").remove();
             
         }
     }
 
     function prepareBreadcrumb(breadcrumbData){
 
         if (breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs && breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs.length > 0) {
 
             var breadcrumbTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#breadcrumb-template").html());
             $("div.breadcrumb-main").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             breadcrumbData.isMobile=true;
             $("nav#breadcrumbWrapperMobile").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareSocialShare(socialShareData){
         if (socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration && socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration.length > 0) {
 
             var socialShareTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#social-share-template").html());
             $(".menuFlyout .sh").append(socialShareTemplate(socialShareData));
         }else {
             $(".social-share-menu").remove();
             $(".social-share-desktop").remove();
         }
     }
     
     $(document).ready(function(){
     		PwcCookieConsent.insertScriptFromString('prepareSocialShare(socialShareData);', 'social-share-div',
 				4, null, null, null, null, null, true);
     })
      </script>

                 <h3 class="h4 regular collection__item-heading">
                  Datenschutz: Neue Regeln, neue Aufgaben
                 </h3>
                 <p class="collection__item-paragraph">
                  Datenschutz gehört in Unternehmen zu den Schlüsselthemen und wird mehr Bedeutung erlangen. Denn zum einen tritt die EU-Datenschutz-Grundverordnung am 25. Mai 2018 in Kraft. Zum anderen befindet sich das schweizerische Datenschutzgesetz in Revision und wird voraussichtlich im 2019 in Kraft treten.
                 </p>

   <script>
    function getCookie(cname) {
             var name = cname + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                 if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
             }
             return "";
         }
         function redirect(redirectToURL) {
             var redirect = 'null';
             if (redirectToURL != null && redirectToURL.trim().length > 0) {
                 redirect = redirectToURL;
             }
             if (window.location.hash) {
                 redirect += window.location.hash;
             }
             if (redirect != 'null') {
                 window.location.replace(redirect);
             }
         }

      <script>
       var socialShareData;
     
 	if (showLanguageSelector) {
 		prepareLanguageSelector(navigationData.languageSelectorData);
 	}    
 	prepareTerritorySelector(navigationData.territorySelectorData);
     prepareHamburger(navigationData.hamburgerData);
     prepareBreadcrumb(navigationData.breadcrumbData);
     socialShareData = navigationData.socialShareData;
     function createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             var languageListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#language-selector-template").html());
             $("#menuAdditional .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             languageSelectorData.isMobile=true;
             $("#menuAdditionalMobile .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
         }
     }
 
     function  prepareLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             //render alternate language div on page only if alternate language present on page/slim-header.
             createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData);
         }
     }
 
     function prepareTerritorySelector(territories){
         if (territories && territories.length > 0) {
             var territoryListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#territory-selector-template").html());
             $(".territory-dropdown").append(territoryListTemplate(territories));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareHamburger(hamburgerData){
         if ((hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks && (hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0
                 || hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0)) || (hamburgerData.levelOneLinks && hamburgerData.levelOneLinks.length > 0)) {
 
            
             if(hamburgerData.sectionTitle){
                 hamburgerData.hasSectionTitle=true;
             }
            // modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary);
             //modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.secondary);
             var hamburgerTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-template").html());
             //$("div.breadcrumb-main").append(hamburgerTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             $(".hamburger-menu .col-sm-8").append(hamburgerTemplate(hamburgerData));
             //populate levelOne links of hamburger
             var hamburgerLevelOneTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-levelOne-template").html());
             $("#LevelOneLinks").prepend(hamburgerLevelOneTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
             //populate hamburger for mobile
             var hamburgerMobileTemplate= Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-mobile-template").html());
             $(".hamburger-submenu--mobile .panel-group").append(hamburgerMobileTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
         }else {
             //if levelOne or LevelTwo or LevelThree Links are not present, hamburger button should not be shown.
             $("#dropdownTrigger_lg").remove();
             $("#navBar").remove();
             
         }
     }
 
     function prepareBreadcrumb(breadcrumbData){
 
         if (breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs && breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs.length > 0) {
 
             var breadcrumbTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#breadcrumb-template").html());
             $("div.breadcrumb-main").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             breadcrumbData.isMobile=true;
             $("nav#breadcrumbWrapperMobile").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareSocialShare(socialShareData){
         if (socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration && socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration.length > 0) {
 
             var socialShareTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#social-share-template").html());
             $(".menuFlyout .sh").append(socialShareTemplate(socialShareData));
         }else {
             $(".social-share-menu").remove();
             $(".social-share-desktop").remove();
         }
     }
     
     $(document).ready(function(){
     		PwcCookieConsent.insertScriptFromString('prepareSocialShare(socialShareData);', 'social-share-div',
 				4, null, null, null, null, null, true);
     })
      </script>

                 </h3>
                 <p class="collection__item-paragraph">
                  Datenschutz gehört in Unternehmen zu den Schlüsselthemen und wird mehr Bedeutung erlangen. Denn zum einen tritt die EU-Datenschutz-Grundverordnung am 25. Mai 2018 in Kraft. Zum anderen befindet sich das schweizerische Datenschutzgesetz in Revision und wird voraussichtlich im 2019 in Kraft treten.
                 </p>
                 <div>

    function getCookie(cname) {
             var name = cname + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                 if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
             }
             return "";
         }
         function redirect(redirectToURL) {
             var redirect = 'null';
             if (redirectToURL != null && redirectToURL.trim().length > 0) {
                 redirect = redirectToURL;
             }
             if (window.location.hash) {
                 redirect += window.location.hash;
             }
             if (redirect != 'null') {
                 window.location.replace(redirect);
             }
         }

      <script>
       var socialShareData;
     
 	if (showLanguageSelector) {
 		prepareLanguageSelector(navigationData.languageSelectorData);
 	}    
 	prepareTerritorySelector(navigationData.territorySelectorData);
     prepareHamburger(navigationData.hamburgerData);
     prepareBreadcrumb(navigationData.breadcrumbData);
     socialShareData = navigationData.socialShareData;
     function createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             var languageListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#language-selector-template").html());
             $("#menuAdditional .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             languageSelectorData.isMobile=true;
             $("#menuAdditionalMobile .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
         }
     }
 
     function  prepareLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             //render alternate language div on page only if alternate language present on page/slim-header.
             createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData);
         }
     }
 
     function prepareTerritorySelector(territories){
         if (territories && territories.length > 0) {
             var territoryListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#territory-selector-template").html());
             $(".territory-dropdown").append(territoryListTemplate(territories));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareHamburger(hamburgerData){
         if ((hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks && (hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0
                 || hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0)) || (hamburgerData.levelOneLinks && hamburgerData.levelOneLinks.length > 0)) {
 
            
             if(hamburgerData.sectionTitle){
                 hamburgerData.hasSectionTitle=true;
             }
            // modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary);
             //modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.secondary);
             var hamburgerTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-template").html());
             //$("div.breadcrumb-main").append(hamburgerTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             $(".hamburger-menu .col-sm-8").append(hamburgerTemplate(hamburgerData));
             //populate levelOne links of hamburger
             var hamburgerLevelOneTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-levelOne-template").html());
             $("#LevelOneLinks").prepend(hamburgerLevelOneTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
             //populate hamburger for mobile
             var hamburgerMobileTemplate= Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-mobile-template").html());
             $(".hamburger-submenu--mobile .panel-group").append(hamburgerMobileTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
         }else {
             //if levelOne or LevelTwo or LevelThree Links are not present, hamburger button should not be shown.
             $("#dropdownTrigger_lg").remove();
             $("#navBar").remove();
             
         }
     }
 
     function prepareBreadcrumb(breadcrumbData){
 
         if (breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs && breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs.length > 0) {
 
             var breadcrumbTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#breadcrumb-template").html());
             $("div.breadcrumb-main").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             breadcrumbData.isMobile=true;
             $("nav#breadcrumbWrapperMobile").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareSocialShare(socialShareData){
         if (socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration && socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration.length > 0) {
 
             var socialShareTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#social-share-template").html());
             $(".menuFlyout .sh").append(socialShareTemplate(socialShareData));
         }else {
             $(".social-share-menu").remove();
             $(".social-share-desktop").remove();
         }
     }
     
     $(document).ready(function(){
     		PwcCookieConsent.insertScriptFromString('prepareSocialShare(socialShareData);', 'social-share-div',
 				4, null, null, null, null, null, true);
     })
      </script>
      <div id="social-share-div">
      </div>

                </div>
                <div class="collection__item-content">
                 <p class="collection__item-sub-heading">
                  <time datetime="26 Jun 2018">
                   26 Jun 2018
                  </time>
                 </p>
                 <h3 class="h4 regular collection__item-heading">
                  Datenschutz: Neue Regeln, neue Aufgaben
                 </h3>
                 <p class="collection__item-paragraph">
                  Datenschutz gehört in Unternehmen zu den Schlüsselthemen und wird mehr Bedeutung erlangen. Denn zum einen tritt die EU-Datenschutz-Grundverordnung am 25. Mai 2018 in Kraft. Zum anderen befindet sich das schweizerische Datenschutzgesetz in Revision und wird voraussichtlich im 2019 in Kraft treten.
                 </p>

   <script>
    function getCookie(cname) {
             var name = cname + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                 if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
             }
             return "";
         }
         function redirect(redirectToURL) {
             var redirect = 'null';
             if (redirectToURL != null && redirectToURL.trim().length > 0) {
                 redirect = redirectToURL;
             }
             if (window.location.hash) {
                 redirect += window.location.hash;
             }
             if (redirect != 'null') {
                 window.location.replace(redirect);
             }
         }

      <script>
       var socialShareData;
     
 	if (showLanguageSelector) {
 		prepareLanguageSelector(navigationData.languageSelectorData);
 	}    
 	prepareTerritorySelector(navigationData.territorySelectorData);
     prepareHamburger(navigationData.hamburgerData);
     prepareBreadcrumb(navigationData.breadcrumbData);
     socialShareData = navigationData.socialShareData;
     function createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             var languageListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#language-selector-template").html());
             $("#menuAdditional .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             languageSelectorData.isMobile=true;
             $("#menuAdditionalMobile .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
         }
     }
 
     function  prepareLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             //render alternate language div on page only if alternate language present on page/slim-header.
             createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData);
         }
     }
 
     function prepareTerritorySelector(territories){
         if (territories && territories.length > 0) {
             var territoryListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#territory-selector-template").html());
             $(".territory-dropdown").append(territoryListTemplate(territories));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareHamburger(hamburgerData){
         if ((hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks && (hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0
                 || hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0)) || (hamburgerData.levelOneLinks && hamburgerData.levelOneLinks.length > 0)) {
 
            
             if(hamburgerData.sectionTitle){
                 hamburgerData.hasSectionTitle=true;
             }
            // modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary);
             //modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.secondary);
             var hamburgerTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-template").html());
             //$("div.breadcrumb-main").append(hamburgerTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             $(".hamburger-menu .col-sm-8").append(hamburgerTemplate(hamburgerData));
             //populate levelOne links of hamburger
             var hamburgerLevelOneTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-levelOne-template").html());
             $("#LevelOneLinks").prepend(hamburgerLevelOneTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
             //populate hamburger for mobile
             var hamburgerMobileTemplate= Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-mobile-template").html());
             $(".hamburger-submenu--mobile .panel-group").append(hamburgerMobileTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
         }else {
             //if levelOne or LevelTwo or LevelThree Links are not present, hamburger button should not be shown.
             $("#dropdownTrigger_lg").remove();
             $("#navBar").remove();
             
         }
     }
 
     function prepareBreadcrumb(breadcrumbData){
 
         if (breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs && breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs.length > 0) {
 
             var breadcrumbTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#breadcrumb-template").html());
             $("div.breadcrumb-main").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             breadcrumbData.isMobile=true;
             $("nav#breadcrumbWrapperMobile").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareSocialShare(socialShareData){
         if (socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration && socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration.length > 0) {
 
             var socialShareTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#social-share-template").html());
             $(".menuFlyout .sh").append(socialShareTemplate(socialShareData));
         }else {
             $(".social-share-menu").remove();
             $(".social-share-desktop").remove();
         }
     }
     
     $(document).ready(function(){
     		PwcCookieConsent.insertScriptFromString('prepareSocialShare(socialShareData);', 'social-share-div',
 				4, null, null, null, null, null, true);
     })
      </script>

   <script>
    function getCookie(cname) {
             var name = cname + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                 if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
             }
             return "";
         }
         function redirect(redirectToURL) {
             var redirect = 'null';
             if (redirectToURL != null && redirectToURL.trim().length > 0) {
                 redirect = redirectToURL;
             }
             if (window.location.hash) {
                 redirect += window.location.hash;
             }
             if (redirect != 'null') {
                 window.location.replace(redirect);
             }
         }

      <script>
       var socialShareData;
     
 	if (showLanguageSelector) {
 		prepareLanguageSelector(navigationData.languageSelectorData);
 	}    
 	prepareTerritorySelector(navigationData.territorySelectorData);
     prepareHamburger(navigationData.hamburgerData);
     prepareBreadcrumb(navigationData.breadcrumbData);
     socialShareData = navigationData.socialShareData;
     function createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages && languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             var languageListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#language-selector-template").html());
             $("#menuAdditional .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             languageSelectorData.isMobile=true;
             $("#menuAdditionalMobile .language-selector-li").append(languageListTemplate(languageSelectorData));
         }
     }
 
     function  prepareLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData){
         if (languageSelectorData.alternateLanguages.length > 0) {
             //render alternate language div on page only if alternate language present on page/slim-header.
             createLanguageSelector(languageSelectorData);
         }
     }
 
     function prepareTerritorySelector(territories){
         if (territories && territories.length > 0) {
             var territoryListTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#territory-selector-template").html());
             $(".territory-dropdown").append(territoryListTemplate(territories));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareHamburger(hamburgerData){
         if ((hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks && (hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0
                 || hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary.length > 0)) || (hamburgerData.levelOneLinks && hamburgerData.levelOneLinks.length > 0)) {
 
            
             if(hamburgerData.sectionTitle){
                 hamburgerData.hasSectionTitle=true;
             }
            // modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.primary);
             //modifyLinks(hamburgerData.hamburgerLinks.secondary);
             var hamburgerTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-template").html());
             //$("div.breadcrumb-main").append(hamburgerTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             $(".hamburger-menu .col-sm-8").append(hamburgerTemplate(hamburgerData));
             //populate levelOne links of hamburger
             var hamburgerLevelOneTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-levelOne-template").html());
             $("#LevelOneLinks").prepend(hamburgerLevelOneTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
             //populate hamburger for mobile
             var hamburgerMobileTemplate= Handlebars.compile($("#hamburger-mobile-template").html());
             $(".hamburger-submenu--mobile .panel-group").append(hamburgerMobileTemplate(hamburgerData));
             
         }else {
             //if levelOne or LevelTwo or LevelThree Links are not present, hamburger button should not be shown.
             $("#dropdownTrigger_lg").remove();
             $("#navBar").remove();
             
         }
     }
 
     function prepareBreadcrumb(breadcrumbData){
 
         if (breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs && breadcrumbData.breadcrumbs.length > 0) {
 
             var breadcrumbTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#breadcrumb-template").html());
             $("div.breadcrumb-main").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
 
             //prepare markup for mobile
             breadcrumbData.isMobile=true;
             $("nav#breadcrumbWrapperMobile").append(breadcrumbTemplate(breadcrumbData));
         }
     }
 
     function prepareSocialShare(socialShareData){
         if (socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration && socialShareData.socialShareConfiguration.length > 0) {
 
             var socialShareTemplate = Handlebars.compile($("#social-share-template").html());
             $(".menuFlyout .sh").append(socialShareTemplate(socialShareData));
         }else {
             $(".social-share-menu").remove();
             $(".social-share-desktop").remove();
         }
     }
     
     $(document).ready(function(){
     		PwcCookieConsent.insertScriptFromString('prepareSocialShare(socialShareData);', 'social-share-div',
 				4, null, null, null, null, null, true);
     })
      </script>

                <div class="collection__item-image-wrapper">
                 <img alt="Datenschutz: Neue Regeln, neue Aufgaben" class="img-responsive" src="/de/images/image/bridge_1600x900.jpg/jcr:content/renditions/cq5dam.thumbnail.319.319.png"/>
                </div>
                <div class="collection__item-content">
                 <p class="collection__item-sub-heading">
                  <time datetime="26 Jun 2018">
                   26 Jun 2018
                  </time>
                 </p>
                 <h3 class="h4 regular collection__item-heading">
                  Datenschutz: Neue Regeln, neue Aufgaben
                 </h3>
                 <p class="collection__item-paragraph">
                  Datenschutz gehört in Unternehmen zu den Schlüsselthemen und wird mehr Bedeutung erlangen. Denn zum einen tritt die EU-Datenschutz-Grundverordnung am 25. Mai 2018 in Kraft. Zum anderen befindet sich das schweizerische Datenschutzgesetz in Revision und wird voraussichtlich im 2019 in Kraft treten.
                 </p>
                 <div>
